<userid>117716344127323504461<//userid>< review>
I liked this park because it has 2 full sized basketball courts, and a big grass field for baseball, soccer, football, etc... They also, which is very rare, have a vending machine which gives Gatorade and this is the first time I have seen this at a public park. However, they need to work on having more water fountains, there is only one, and a bigger playground for small kids. Overall, a great place for family...</review>

<Rating>5< /Rating>< Text>
Wonderful place for some Italian grub!

We ordered the Pepperoni Pizza, Chicken Wings, and a couple of desserts (Cannoli and Cheesecake).

Everything was satisfactory, if not absolutely amazing!! The pepperoni pizza was SO GOOD. Not greasy... lovely sauce... and LARGE pepperonis. Perfectly cooked crust.

The chicken wings were great! They come in 12pc, but they were a little small... and there were definitely more than 12 in the container... so that was cool.

The Cannoli dessert came with 4 mini ricotta cannolis. Very good! I'm not usually a fan of lemon, but these were actually really good! And we got the cheesecake. Can't go wrong. Drizzled in strawberries. Fabulous!

Great experience! Happy we found this place! Can't wait to visit again!< /Text>

<text>It has been several years since my last visit. I have been back three times in one week because everything I try is so good! <time>1541872671455<//time><Rating>5< /Rating><Review>If you like the subtle taste of home made Italian food, this is the best hidden treasure in Los Angeles.  And that's not hyperbole.  It's fact.  Starting with their New York style pizza, with its just right crust, whole milk mozzarella and perfectly sweet tomato sauce, all the way to the "linguine alle vongole veraci," with its rich buttery, garlic broth it's like home made, like grandmother made.  I mean that only if your grandmother were a real good, nay, great Italian cook.  My wife and I have eaten our way through most of the menu and haven't found one item disappointing. < Review>
I used to go here very frequently as I lived just a stone's throw away, and it WAS one of my favourite Italian restaurants in West Hollywood, but it has turned into such a SORRY ESTABLISHMENT that you'll literally get better service at McDonald's. Most of the Staff that's presently there is *ABOMINABLE*. My last couple of visits left a lot to be desired, but just last night, I met the ABSOLUTE WORST SERVER I have ever encountered in this world (and I've travelled to over 25 countries, including Italy of course).

This MISERABLY ILL-BRED man, Alessandro, had neither a greeting nor a smile, and after I asked for some water to start with, the miscreant proceeds to spend a good 7 minutes at the very next table taking about himself to the 2 middle-aged women seated there, and actually trying to persuade one of them to leave her boyfriend (The woman seemed vaguely amused throughout all this, and politely affirmed that she had no such intention). Several minutes passed after this odious conversation, and the man showed absolutely no signs of wanting to take my order. There were a number of other people working at the restaurant, but this was the only person doing the rounds for whatever reason. I finally caught his attention and asked him, in a very even tone, whether he could PLEASE take my order. The idiot says Yes, and then proceeds to VANISH OUT OF SIGHT to the back of the restaurant.

5 minutes later (a.k.a nearly 15 minutes after I first sat down), I arose from the table, complained to one of the workers standing by the counter that NO ONE HAD TAKEN MY ORDER, and left the place. The worker I complained to, who definitely spoke English as I heard him on the phone earlier, stood there mute and nonplussed, along with one of the bus-boys. No apologies, NOTHING.

I called afterwards and asked for the Manager - the first person who answered the phone put me on hold and never returned to the phone. I called back, someone else picked up and claimed that the Manager wasn't there, and that they didn't know when he WOULD be there, but that his name was Bernardo (who knows). I'm not going to let this go, and since I often visit the Burke Williams Spa that's round the corner, I intend to speak to someone in charge over the next couple of weeks.

Suffice it to say, please do not even *THINK* of going here. Alessandro the waiter is a *DISGRACE TO ITALY*, and should be relegated to doing the dishes if he's incapable of even TAKING DOWN A PATRON'S ORDER (apparently one has to be a middle-aged woman to capture his attention. Disgusting!!!!!!)<//Review>

< review>
I highly recommend this place if you're really hungry. The all you can eat and the all you can eat AND drink deals are amazing. The spicy miso broth and ginger chicken are the famous broths (order half and half to get both). If it's your first time to shabu/hot pot you can always ask for help or read the instructions on the plastic table sign. They have other food items for those that are not really adventurous. Great location and easily commutable.</review>

<Rate>5< /Rate><username>Jimmy Keener< /username><Pictures>None< /Pictures>< time>

< review>
Excellent Plumbing contractor, responsive, and quick professional inexpensive service. We had our whole house sewer back up from the front of the house clean out. This should have been a quick job. I tried to call a few companies Thursday between 10:00 pm and1:00 am, only one company responded, and they wanted $500 for immediate service or $275 Friday morning. I said No, and Friday morning rented an auger machine from Home Depot for $75. When I opened the clean out in the front of the house, the water had receded over night, i could see water at the bottom and i saw there was an opening headed away from the house towards the street. I added water to see if it had cleared, no luck. I pushed cable through the line, slowly. When I met an obstruction i backed off let it idle in place to "chew" on the obstruction before pushing forward. I wasn't making very much progress. My home is only 12 years old, and I have no trees in my front yard. As I worked i kept wondering where all these roots were coming from. My wife came out several times informing me she heard banging in the pipes; I dismissed her concerns telling her it is just echoes, and kept going. After SEVERAL HOURS I had only succeeded in pushing about 50 feet of cable into the system. Still not cleared. I pulled the cable out and found the cable tip was missing. I took the uager back to Home Depot and got a different machine. I started again. Working slowly, feeding the cable, idling, backing up and moving forward. This time i used a large cutting bit. We were in the middle of a heat wave and California was burning down causing smoke to fill the sky, up and down the central valley of the state. My wife brought a fan tower out for me to get cool...a little. After an hour or so I was successful in feeding all 100 feet of 5/8" cable into the system. Still not clear, i called the city, they checked their system and it was clear. I was about 25 feet shy of the manhole. I tried to call American Home Shield but couldn't get through. So I found PDS Plumbing on Yelp; a veteran owned and operated local family business. I spoke with Daniel, explained our situation, and the fact we couldn't use any of our restrooms for the past day and a half (my daughter owns a home around the corner), Daniel said he had a guy he could send out in the next hour. He said because I was retired Law Enforcement as well as a disabled veteran he would provide a great discount and thanked me for my service. JosÃ©, Daniel and Dan all arrived at the expected time. They all had PPE on, including face masks and were very careful regarding distancing due to the Wuhan virus. They accessed the front of the house clean out and began to work. I explained to them I believed the clean out had a 90 degree end headed towards the street. They quickly ran the cable to the back yard clean out...what? Okay so now they knew it was a 2 way, they pulled the cable back out and cleared the line about 10 feet in front of my house. Daniel scoped my mainline and discovered a sagging line. He further advised me, if I have problems in the future make sure the auger goes through the rear of the house clean out, that way I know I'm going the right direction. But...where is the cable tip that I lost in the system?  Lesson learned, my wife is most often right.< /review>

< Review>
Probably the best view over the city and Golden Gate bridge in this part of the city. Features 4 tennis courts, a tennis pratice wall and 2 basket ball hoops. Playing here is free, but you might have to wait a bit for a vacancy.

If you just want to enjoy the view and take a picture, you can usually sneak in if it's ok with the people playing.</Review>

Quentin Wright<//name>
<Resp>None< /Resp>< Text>
From a Vendor point of view: Wednesday's space fee is way overpriced @ $25. Hardly any customers show up. Vendors are allowed to sell fake name brands such as Michael Kors, Adidas, Nike Pink as well as others and none of the staff says anything. This makes it really hard on the vendors who go out and by the real items and try to complete reselling against the fakes. Not Right and its illegal. The management of the Madera flea market should consider advertising more or doing something to draw more customers in and make it a better experience for all. It's time to stop raking in the money and telling all the vendors what they can't do and maybe try telling the vendors what you have done for them since they're the only reason that the entire flea market is open. Everybody steps on the little guy until he becomes your boss. On a positive note the food is great the vegetables look fabulous and most of the vendors are pretty nice, even most of the staff seem to have a real positive attitude.

I tell one, I tell all, come support the vendors at all the flea markets. Come and have a great time. Come and eat some delicious food. Take home some very unique and fabulous items. But remember the vendors work hard to pick, front the cash and buy this stuff for you. They can't sell it at a cheaper price than they paid, so please be considerate in your negotiations and don't insult a vendor buy offering half the price,  that they are asking. If you can't come somewhat close to their asking price  just being nice say thank you and move on. You have so many choices  that you don't have to insult the vendor, just a little word of advice.<//Text>

< Review>
One busy place on Sunday. The Wed event is smaller, Sunday is huge. Mostly low quality clothing and such, but lots of good produce and hard to find seasonings and cooking stuff. The cheap new clothing is overpriced and isn't worth your hard earned money. Even had a Santa booth for the kiddos to take pics with him, and mini horse rides and even masseuse services. Lotta good food. Costs two bucks each person to get in. Very little of what is usually thought of for a swap meet, people selling their old stuff like tools or lawn furniture or whatever, it's almost all vendors with new stuff. You can do better buying most things online or at Wal-Mart as far as prices and quality go, but a fun time and place.<//Review>
